SpliveMc - Update!
badsk = Layer
Latest badsk/Layer hosting = CitricNode - https://citricnode.com
It's a Minecraft hosting, however it offers Debian VMs
It's very easy to break it - make a Debian server, wait for it to install then do fallocate -l 9999G ./diskfill
After some time your server will stop, and the node you did this on will be full. That means if you do that on USA node, no one will be able to make a server in USA

Their companies are really registered:
Sryden - https://find-and-update.company-information.service.gov.uk/search?q=Sryden
CitricNode - https://find-and-update.company-information.service.gov.uk/company/05773814
